**App for IOS system devices (mobile phone/iPad)**

1.  Open App Store.
    
    [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/27924fdb3d67692df7c63d8d0fb72287.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/27924fdb3d67692df7c63d8d0fb72287.png)
    
2.  Enter “keyes wifi” in the search box, search and the download screen will appear. Click“[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/962a57f92b78eea1f0e3e81463497a9c.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/962a57f92b78eea1f0e3e81463497a9c.png)”，b., you can download and install keyes wifi APP. The following operations are similar to those of Android system. You can refer to the steps of Android system above for operation.
    

Note: Click the button on APP, the blue light on ESP8266 serial WiFi ESP-01 module will flash, indicating that APP has connected to WiFi.

After the APP has been connected to the WiFi, start the following operations.

1.  Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/5b9754cb6ec4f995c9eada1da89a8969.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/5b9754cb6ec4f995c9eada1da89a8969.png).Relay opens and the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/505b00b0e23f6498c5d51d5d775c8fcb.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/505b00b0e23f6498c5d51d5d775c8fcb.png),the indicator light on the module lights up. Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/5b9754cb6ec4f995c9eada1da89a8969.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/5b9754cb6ec4f995c9eada1da89a8969.png) again, relay is closed and the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/deb54a77cdcc87d7569e8b8e46de129f.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/deb54a77cdcc87d7569e8b8e46de129f.png), indicator light on the module goes out.
    
2.  Click[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/c54f78d819d4e6a8310eaeb79ff66910.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/c54f78d819d4e6a8310eaeb79ff66910.png). The servo rotates 180° and the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/d6feecf1992cbaf09f03c20b5b7f5414.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/d6feecf1992cbaf09f03c20b5b7f5414.png). Click[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/c54f78d819d4e6a8310eaeb79ff66910.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/c54f78d819d4e6a8310eaeb79ff66910.png)again, the APP shows [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/dee12bee3866542bfe5d70a539f79f0b.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/dee12bee3866542bfe5d70a539f79f0b.png)，the servo rotates 0°.
    
3.  Click[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/5490abf5b2f8a1d9cea3055da07c251c.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/5490abf5b2f8a1d9cea3055da07c251c.png). Motor (with small fan leaves)rotates and the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/e609128934bc72a89b39ded5833d050e.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/e609128934bc72a89b39ded5833d050e.png). Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/5490abf5b2f8a1d9cea3055da07c251c.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/5490abf5b2f8a1d9cea3055da07c251c.png) again. Turn off the motor, the APP shows [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/4f450510172cdd7c4d8a7c6b39881a90.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/4f450510172cdd7c4d8a7c6b39881a90.png).
    
4.  Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/95bfbe879d2391e4e48dcae085abe5a6.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/95bfbe879d2391e4e48dcae085abe5a6.png), ultrasonic sensor measures distance. Put an object in front of the ultrasonic sensor, and the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/676c8a750e95c84272b0b7791f7b3cd3.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/676c8a750e95c84272b0b7791f7b3cd3.png)（Different distance shows different numbers). It means that the distance of the object from the ultrasonic sensor is 14cm at this time. Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/95bfbe879d2391e4e48dcae085abe5a6.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/95bfbe879d2391e4e48dcae085abe5a6.png). Turn off ultrasound, the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/b1df35af68601022e54b7e575b0a07c7.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/b1df35af68601022e54b7e575b0a07c7.png).
    
5.  Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/08c8a35841b31fa4b5327fb7b23a7af5.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/08c8a35841b31fa4b5327fb7b23a7af5.png),temperature and humidity sensor measures the temperature in the environment. The APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/2a40f3e895808a3c6d4e1f542133feba.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/2a40f3e895808a3c6d4e1f542133feba.png), which means that the temperature in the environment is 28℃ at this time. Click[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/08c8a35841b31fa4b5327fb7b23a7af5.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/08c8a35841b31fa4b5327fb7b23a7af5.png), turn off the temperature and humidity sensor, the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/82887a1385bc7411ecbdc41f60ebd450.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/82887a1385bc7411ecbdc41f60ebd450.png).
    
6.  Click [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/d8e3463ab2f644b3300cdeaa2a68e4c2.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/d8e3463ab2f644b3300cdeaa2a68e4c2.png), temperature and humidity sensor measures the humidity in the environment. The APP shows [![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/cc825e69cf073aa73e37712330f4726e.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/cc825e69cf073aa73e37712330f4726e.png), it means that the humidity in the environment is 52% at this time. Click[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/d8e3463ab2f644b3300cdeaa2a68e4c2.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/d8e3463ab2f644b3300cdeaa2a68e4c2.png)，turn off the temperature and humidity sensor, the APP shows[![](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/raw/master/media/adc18d06e626af067286da9040c20252.png)](https://github.com/keyestudio/KS0536-KS0537--Keyestudio-Ultimate-Starter-Kit-for-Arduino/blob/master/media/adc18d06e626af067286da9040c20252.png).
